      <meta name="voltron-timing" value="734">
    <script type="application/ld+json">{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"DiscussionForumPosting","headline":"Incomplete fix for CVE-2026-0994: Struct/Value/ListValue mutual recursion bypasses max_recursion_depth","articleBody":"\n[protobuf-recursion-poc.zip](https://github.com/user-attachments/files/26071747/protobuf-recursion-poc.zip)\n\n\u003chtml\u003e\u003chead\u003e\u003c/head\u003e\u003cbody\u003e\u003ch1\u003eIncomplete fix for CVE-2026-0994: \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eValue\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eListValue\u003c/code\u003e mutual recursion bypasses \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e in Python JSON parser\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eSummary\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe fix for CVE-2026-0994 (GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7) patched \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertAnyMessage\u003c/code\u003e by\nrouting it through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e, which increments \u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e.\nHowever, the identical pattern remains unfixed in three other methods:\n\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertValueMessage\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertStructMessage\u003c/code\u003e, and\n\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage\u003c/code\u003e. These methods call each other in a mutual\nrecursion cycle without ever passing through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e, so\n\u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e never advances past \u003ccode\u003e1\u003c/code\u003e. The \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e\nparameter is completely inert for these well-known types.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eConfirmed vulnerable: \u003cstrong\u003e6.33.5\u003c/strong\u003e (the CVE-2026-0994 patched release) and\n\u003cstrong\u003e7.34.0\u003c/strong\u003e (latest as of this report).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eRoot cause\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFile: \u003ccode\u003epython/google/protobuf/json_format.py\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e (line 531) is the sole location that increments\n\u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e. The three WKT conversion methods call each other\ndirectly, bypassing this increment:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertStructMessage            (line 778)\n_ConvertStructMessage     → _ConvertValueMessage             (line 818)\n_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage  (line 780)\n_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage → _ConvertValueMessage       (line 804)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe result: a caller that sets \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth=10\u003c/code\u003e and parses a\n\u003ccode\u003egoogle.protobuf.Struct\u003c/code\u003e from untrusted JSON receives \u003cstrong\u003eno protection\u003c/strong\u003e.\nParsing succeeds at depth 100, 200, 500, … until Python's own default\nrecursion limit (~1 000) is hit, at which point the process raises an\nunhandled \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eReproduction\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003efrom google.protobuf import json_format, struct_pb2\n\n# ~2 KB payload, 500 levels deep\nnested = {\"leaf\": \"data\"}\nfor _ in range(500):\n    nested = {\"level\": nested}\n\nmsg = struct_pb2.Struct()\n\n# max_recursion_depth=10 should reject this immediately.\n# Instead it crashes with RecursionError.\njson_format.ParseDict(nested, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eExpected: \u003ccode\u003ejson_format.ParseError\u003c/code\u003e raised at depth 10.\u003cbr\u003e\nActual: \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e (Python stack exhausted, worker process crashes).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAll four type variants are affected (see attached PoC for full test suite):\u003c/p\u003e\n\nType | Depth 100, limit 10 | Depth 500, limit 10\n-- | -- | --\nStruct | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\nValue | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\nListValue | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eProposed fix\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAdd the same depth guard used by \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e to each of the three\noffending methods. The \u003ccode\u003etry/finally\u003c/code\u003e is required so that a mid-parse\nexception does not leave the counter permanently incremented.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003edef _ConvertStructMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\n\ndef _ConvertValueMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\n\ndef _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA ready-to-apply patch is attached to this issue.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eImpact\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003egoogle.protobuf.Struct\u003c/code\u003e is the standard representation for arbitrary JSON\nin gRPC APIs. Google Cloud services (Dialogflow intents, Firestore documents,\nCloud Functions event payloads) and countless third-party gRPC services\naccept \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e fields from untrusted callers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAny service that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eaccepts a \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eValue\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode\u003eListValue\u003c/code\u003e field from untrusted input, \u003cstrong\u003eand\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ecalls \u003ccode\u003eParseDict\u003c/code\u003e (or \u003ccode\u003eParse\u003c/code\u003e) with an explicit \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e…believes it is protected against deeply-nested payloads. It is not.\nA single ~2 KB HTTP/gRPC request crashes one Python worker. Sending the\nsame request in a loop achieves full service outage.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eReferences\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCVE-2026-0994 / GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7 — original Any bypass\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFix commit for CVE-2026-0994 (routes \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertAnyMessage\u003c/code\u003e through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003epython/google/protobuf/json_format.py\u003c/code\u003e lines 775–821\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWorkaround\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUntil a patch is released, services can enforce a depth limit at the transport\nlayer (e.g. validate JSON depth before calling \u003ccode\u003eParseDict\u003c/code\u003e) or wrap the call\nand catch \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e explicitly:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003eimport sys\n\nold_limit = sys.getrecursionlimit()\nsys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit // 2)   # tighten the safety net\ntry:\n    json_format.ParseDict(data, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)\nexcept RecursionError:\n    raise ValueError(\"Input too deeply nested\")\nfinally:\n    sys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNote: this is not a proper fix—it merely converts the crash into a catchable\nexception. Apply the patch above for a correct solution.\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/body\u003e\u003c/html\u003e","author":{"url":"https://github.com/geoo115","@type":"Person","name":"geoo115"},"datePublished":"2026-03-18T00:14:56.000Z","interactionStatistic":{"@type":"InteractionCounter","interactionType":"https://schema.org/CommentAction","userInteractionCount":0},"url":"https://github.com/26432/protobuf/issues/26432"}</script>

  data-react-profiling="false"
>
  
  <script type="application/json" data-target="react-app.embeddedData">{"payload":{"preloaded_records":{},"structured_data":{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"DiscussionForumPosting","headline":"Incomplete fix for CVE-2026-0994: Struct/Value/ListValue mutual recursion bypasses max_recursion_depth","articleBody":"\n[protobuf-recursion-poc.zip](https://github.com/user-attachments/files/26071747/protobuf-recursion-poc.zip)\n\n\u003chtml\u003e\u003chead\u003e\u003c/head\u003e\u003cbody\u003e\u003ch1\u003eIncomplete fix for CVE-2026-0994: \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eValue\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eListValue\u003c/code\u003e mutual recursion bypasses \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e in Python JSON parser\u003c/h1\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eSummary\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe fix for CVE-2026-0994 (GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7) patched \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertAnyMessage\u003c/code\u003e by\nrouting it through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e, which increments \u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e.\nHowever, the identical pattern remains unfixed in three other methods:\n\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertValueMessage\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertStructMessage\u003c/code\u003e, and\n\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage\u003c/code\u003e. These methods call each other in a mutual\nrecursion cycle without ever passing through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e, so\n\u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e never advances past \u003ccode\u003e1\u003c/code\u003e. The \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e\nparameter is completely inert for these well-known types.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eConfirmed vulnerable: \u003cstrong\u003e6.33.5\u003c/strong\u003e (the CVE-2026-0994 patched release) and\n\u003cstrong\u003e7.34.0\u003c/strong\u003e (latest as of this report).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eRoot cause\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFile: \u003ccode\u003epython/google/protobuf/json_format.py\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e (line 531) is the sole location that increments\n\u003ccode\u003eself.recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e. The three WKT conversion methods call each other\ndirectly, bypassing this increment:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode\u003e_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertStructMessage            (line 778)\n_ConvertStructMessage     → _ConvertValueMessage             (line 818)\n_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage  (line 780)\n_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage → _ConvertValueMessage       (line 804)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe result: a caller that sets \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth=10\u003c/code\u003e and parses a\n\u003ccode\u003egoogle.protobuf.Struct\u003c/code\u003e from untrusted JSON receives \u003cstrong\u003eno protection\u003c/strong\u003e.\nParsing succeeds at depth 100, 200, 500, … until Python's own default\nrecursion limit (~1 000) is hit, at which point the process raises an\nunhandled \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eReproduction\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003efrom google.protobuf import json_format, struct_pb2\n\n# ~2 KB payload, 500 levels deep\nnested = {\"leaf\": \"data\"}\nfor _ in range(500):\n    nested = {\"level\": nested}\n\nmsg = struct_pb2.Struct()\n\n# max_recursion_depth=10 should reject this immediately.\n# Instead it crashes with RecursionError.\njson_format.ParseDict(nested, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eExpected: \u003ccode\u003ejson_format.ParseError\u003c/code\u003e raised at depth 10.\u003cbr\u003e\nActual: \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e (Python stack exhausted, worker process crashes).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAll four type variants are affected (see attached PoC for full test suite):\u003c/p\u003e\n\nType | Depth 100, limit 10 | Depth 500, limit 10\n-- | -- | --\nStruct | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\nValue | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\nListValue | parses — limit bypassed | RecursionError\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eProposed fix\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAdd the same depth guard used by \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage()\u003c/code\u003e to each of the three\noffending methods. The \u003ccode\u003etry/finally\u003c/code\u003e is required so that a mid-parse\nexception does not leave the counter permanently incremented.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003edef _ConvertStructMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\n\ndef _ConvertValueMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\n\ndef _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage(self, value, message):\n    if self.recursion_depth \u0026gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:\n        raise ParseError(\n            \"Message too nested: the value specified for message type \"\n            f\"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested.\"\n        )\n    self.recursion_depth += 1\n    try:\n        # ... existing body unchanged ...\n    finally:\n        self.recursion_depth -= 1\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eA ready-to-apply patch is attached to this issue.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eImpact\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003egoogle.protobuf.Struct\u003c/code\u003e is the standard representation for arbitrary JSON\nin gRPC APIs. Google Cloud services (Dialogflow intents, Firestore documents,\nCloud Functions event payloads) and countless third-party gRPC services\naccept \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e fields from untrusted callers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAny service that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eaccepts a \u003ccode\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eValue\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode\u003eListValue\u003c/code\u003e field from untrusted input, \u003cstrong\u003eand\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ecalls \u003ccode\u003eParseDict\u003c/code\u003e (or \u003ccode\u003eParse\u003c/code\u003e) with an explicit \u003ccode\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e…believes it is protected against deeply-nested payloads. It is not.\nA single ~2 KB HTTP/gRPC request crashes one Python worker. Sending the\nsame request in a loop achieves full service outage.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eReferences\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCVE-2026-0994 / GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7 — original Any bypass\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFix commit for CVE-2026-0994 (routes \u003ccode\u003e_ConvertAnyMessage\u003c/code\u003e through \u003ccode\u003eConvertMessage\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003epython/google/protobuf/json_format.py\u003c/code\u003e lines 775–821\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWorkaround\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUntil a patch is released, services can enforce a depth limit at the transport\nlayer (e.g. validate JSON depth before calling \u003ccode\u003eParseDict\u003c/code\u003e) or wrap the call\nand catch \u003ccode\u003eRecursionError\u003c/code\u003e explicitly:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-python\"\u003eimport sys\n\nold_limit = sys.getrecursionlimit()\nsys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit // 2)   # tighten the safety net\ntry:\n    json_format.ParseDict(data, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)\nexcept RecursionError:\n    raise ValueError(\"Input too deeply nested\")\nfinally:\n    sys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNote: this is not a proper fix—it merely converts the crash into a catchable\nexception. class=\"notranslate\"\u003e_ConvertValueMessage\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003e_ConvertStructMessage\u003c/code\u003e, and\n\u003ccode parses a\n\u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003egoogle.protobuf.Struct\u003c/code\u003e from untrusted JSON receives \u003cstrong\u003eno protection\u003c/strong\u003e.\nParsing succeeds at depth 100, three\noffending methods. Google Cloud services (Dialogflow intents, Firestore documents,\nCloud Functions event payloads) and countless third-party gRPC services\naccept \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e fields from untrusted callers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAny service that:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eaccepts a \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eStruct\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eValue\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eListValue\u003c/code\u003e field from untrusted input, \u003cstrong\u003eand\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ecalls \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eParseDict\u003c/code\u003e (or \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003eParse\u003c/code\u003e) with an explicit \u003ccode class=\"notranslate\"\u003emax_recursion_depth\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e…believes it is protected against deeply-nested payloads. It is not.\nA single ~2 KB HTTP/gRPC request crashes one Python worker. data-testid="issue-body-viewer"><div data-testid="markdown-body" data-team-hovercards-enabled="true" class="markdown-body" data-turbolinks="false"><div class="markdown-body NewMarkdownViewer-module__safe-html-box__ZT1eD"><p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/user-attachments/files/26071747/protobuf-recursion-poc.zip">protobuf-recursion-poc.zip</a></p>
<h1 dir="auto">Incomplete fix for <a title="CVE-2026-0994" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">CVE-2026-0994</a>: <code class="notranslate">Struct</code>/<code class="notranslate">Value</code>/<code class="notranslate">ListValue</code> mutual recursion bypasses <code class="notranslate">max_recursion_depth</code> in Python JSON parser</h1>
<h2 dir="auto">Summary</h2>
<p dir="auto">The fix for <a title="CVE-2026-0994" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">CVE-2026-0994</a> (<a title="GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7</a>) patched <code class="notranslate">_ConvertAnyMessage</code> by
routing it through <code class="notranslate">ConvertMessage()</code>, which increments <code class="notranslate">self.recursion_depth</code>.
However, the identical pattern remains unfixed in three other methods:
<code class="notranslate">_ConvertValueMessage</code>, <code class="notranslate">_ConvertStructMessage</code>, and
<code class="notranslate">_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage</code>. These methods call each other in a mutual
recursion cycle without ever passing through <code class="notranslate">ConvertMessage()</code>, so
<code class="notranslate">self.recursion_depth</code> never advances past <code class="notranslate">1</code>. The <code class="notranslate">max_recursion_depth</code>
parameter is completely inert for these well-known types.</p>
<p dir="auto">Confirmed vulnerable: <strong>6.33.5</strong> (the <a title="CVE-2026-0994" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">CVE-2026-0994</a> patched release) and
<strong>7.34.0</strong> (latest as of this report).</p>
<h2 dir="auto">Root cause</h2>
<p dir="auto">File: <code class="notranslate">python/google/protobuf/json_format.py</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">ConvertMessage()</code> (line 531) is the sole location that increments
<code class="notranslate">self.recursion_depth</code>. The three WKT conversion methods call each other
directly, bypassing this increment:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertStructMessage            (line 778)
_ConvertStructMessage     → _ConvertValueMessage             (line 818)
_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage  (line 780)
_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage → _ConvertValueMessage       (line 804)"><pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertStructMessage            (line 778)
_ConvertStructMessage     → _ConvertValueMessage             (line 818)
_ConvertValueMessage      → _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage  (line 780)
_ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage → _ConvertValueMessage       (line 804)
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The result: a caller that sets <code class="notranslate">max_recursion_depth=10</code> and parses a
<code class="notranslate">google.protobuf.Struct</code> from untrusted JSON receives <strong>no protection</strong>.
Parsing succeeds at depth 100, 200, 500, … until Python's own default
recursion limit (~1 000) is hit, at which point the process raises an
unhandled <code class="notranslate">RecursionError</code>.</p>
<h2 dir="auto">Reproduction</h2>
<pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">from google.protobuf import json_format, struct_pb2
<h1 dir="auto">~2 KB payload, 500 levels deep</h1>
<p dir="auto">nested = {"leaf": "data"}<br>
for _ in range(500):<br>
nested = {"level": nested}</p>
<p dir="auto">msg = struct_pb2.Struct()</p>
<h1 dir="auto">max_recursion_depth=10 should reject this immediately.</h1>
<h1 dir="auto">Instead it crashes with RecursionError.</h1>
</code><p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">json_format.ParseDict(nested, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)<br>
</code></p></pre><p dir="auto"></p>
<p dir="auto">Expected: <code class="notranslate">json_format.ParseError</code> raised at depth 10.<br>
Actual: <code class="notranslate">RecursionError</code> (Python stack exhausted, worker process crashes).</p>
<p dir="auto">All four type variants are affected (see attached PoC for full test suite):</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table role="table">
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Depth 100, limit 10</th>
<th>Depth 500, limit 10</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Struct</td>
<td>parses — limit bypassed</td>
<td>RecursionError</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Value</td>
<td>parses — limit bypassed</td>
<td>RecursionError</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ListValue</td>
<td>parses — limit bypassed</td>
<td>RecursionError</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<h2 dir="auto">Proposed fix</h2>
<p dir="auto">Add the same depth guard used by <code class="notranslate">ConvertMessage()</code> to each of the three
offending methods. The <code class="notranslate">try/finally</code> is required so that a mid-parse
exception does not leave the counter permanently incremented.</p>
<pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">def _ConvertStructMessage(self, value, message):
    if self.recursion_depth &gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:
        raise ParseError(
            "Message too nested: the value specified for message type "
            f"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested."
        )
    self.recursion_depth += 1
    try:
        # ... existing body unchanged ...
    finally:
        self.recursion_depth -= 1
<p dir="auto">def _ConvertValueMessage(self, value, message):<br>
if self.recursion_depth &gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:<br>
raise ParseError(<br>
"Message too nested: the value specified for message type "<br>
f"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested."<br>
)<br>
self.recursion_depth += 1<br>
try:<br>
# ... existing body unchanged ...<br>
finally:<br>
self.recursion_depth -= 1</p>
</code><p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">def _ConvertListOrTupleValueMessage(self, value, message):<br>
if self.recursion_depth &gt;= self.max_recursion_depth:<br>
raise ParseError(<br>
"Message too nested: the value specified for message type "<br>
f"{message.DESCRIPTOR.full_name} is too deeply nested."<br>
)<br>
self.recursion_depth += 1<br>
try:<br>
# ... existing body unchanged ...<br>
finally:<br>
self.recursion_depth -= 1<br>
</code></p></pre><p dir="auto"></p>
<p dir="auto">A ready-to-apply patch is attached to this issue.</p>
<h2 dir="auto">Impact</h2>
<p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">google.protobuf.Struct</code> is the standard representation for arbitrary JSON
in gRPC APIs. Google Cloud services (Dialogflow intents, Firestore documents,
Cloud Functions event payloads) and countless third-party gRPC services
accept <code class="notranslate">Struct</code> fields from untrusted callers.</p>
<p dir="auto">Any service that:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>accepts a <code class="notranslate">Struct</code>, <code class="notranslate">Value</code>, or <code class="notranslate">ListValue</code> field from untrusted input, <strong>and</strong></li>
<li>calls <code class="notranslate">ParseDict</code> (or <code class="notranslate">Parse</code>) with an explicit <code class="notranslate">max_recursion_depth</code></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">…believes it is protected against deeply-nested payloads. It is not.
A single ~2 KB HTTP/gRPC request crashes one Python worker. Sending the
same request in a loop achieves full service outage.</p>
<h2 dir="auto">References</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a title="CVE-2026-0994" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">CVE-2026-0994</a> / <a title="GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7</a> — original Any bypass</li>
<li>Fix commit for <a title="CVE-2026-0994" data-hovercard-type="advisory" data-hovercard-url="/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7/hovercard" href="https://github.com/advisories/GHSA-7gcm-g887-7qv7">CVE-2026-0994</a> (routes <code class="notranslate">_ConvertAnyMessage</code> through <code class="notranslate">ConvertMessage</code>)</li>
<li><code class="notranslate">python/google/protobuf/json_format.py</code> lines 775–821</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto">Workaround</h2>
<p dir="auto">Until a patch is released, services can enforce a depth limit at the transport
layer (e.g. validate JSON depth before calling <code class="notranslate">ParseDict</code>) or wrap the call
and catch <code class="notranslate">RecursionError</code> explicitly:</p>
<pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">import sys
</code><p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">old_limit = sys.getrecursionlimit()<br>
sys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit // 2)   # tighten the safety net<br>
try:<br>
json_format.ParseDict(data, msg, max_recursion_depth=10)<br>
except RecursionError:<br>
raise ValueError("Input too deeply nested")<br>
finally:<br>
sys.setrecursionlimit(old_limit)<br>
</code></p></pre><p dir="auto"></p>
<p dir="auto">Note: this is not a proper fix—it merely converts the crash into a catchable
exception. Apply the patch above for a correct solution.</p></div></div><div class="IssueBodyViewer-module__IssueBodyTaskList__a_Inr"><!--$!--><template></template><button data-component="IconButton"
